      • 0 python -c import sys # split strings by '.' and convert to numeric. Append some zeros # because we need at least 4 digits for the hex conversion. # map returns an iterator in Python 3.0 and a list in 2.x minver = list(map(int, '2.5'.split('.'))) + [0, 0, 0] minverhex = 0 # xrange is not present in Python 3.0 and range returns an iterator for i in list(range(0, 4)): minverhex = (minverhex << 8) + minver[i] sys.exit(sys.hexversion < minverhex)
